/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SavedComplianceList]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SavedComplianceList] 
AS

  Select DISTINCT a.[ComplianceFormID]
      ,FORMAT(a.[CreatedOn],'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss')CreatedOn
	  ,ContractorAssessment.CompanyName
	  ,UserMaster.FirstName+' '+LastName SenderName
	  ,(Select sum(convert(float,b.Quantity)) From WasteMeasure b where b.ComplianceFormID=a.ComplianceFormID )As Quantity
	  ,STUFF((SELECT DISTINCT ',' + b.WasteName FROM WasteMeasure b  WHERE b.ComplianceFormID= a.ComplianceFormID ORDER BY ',' + b.WasteName FOR XML PATH('')), 1, 1, '') AS [WasteName]
	


      
  FROM [dbo].[Compliance] a 
      inner JOIN WasteMeasure b ON a.ComplianceFormID=b.ComplianceFormID

		Join dbo.WasteMeasure   on a.ComplianceFormID=b.ComplianceFormID
		join dbo.[ContractorAssessment] on ContractorAssessment.ContractorID=a.ReceiverName
		join dbo.[UserMaster] on UserMaster.UserID=a.SenderCertificate 
		
	where a.ComplianceFormID=b.ComplianceFormID and a.Status in ('D') 







		
  

 










GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SavedCompliancePDF]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SavedCompliancePDF] 
@ComplianceID int
AS

  Select DISTINCT  a.[ComplianceFormID]
      ,FORMAT(a.[CreatedOn],'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss')CreatedOn
	  ,(select c.CompanyName+','+c.Address+','+c.Street+','+c.City+','+c.PostCode+','+c.MobileNo+','+c.EmailAddress)as TransporterName
	  ,c.TransporterRegistrationNo
	  ,VechicleType.VechicleType
	  ,a.VechicleRegistrationNumber
	  ,(select c1.CompanyName+','+c1.Address+','+c1.Street+','+c1.City+','+c1.PostCode+','+c1.MobileNo+','+c1.EmailAddress)as ReceiverName
	  ,c1.ReceiverAuthorizationNo
	  ,b.WasteName
	  ,(Select sum(convert(float,b.Quantity)) From WasteMeasure b where b.ComplianceFormID=a.ComplianceFormID )As Quantity
	 
	 ,PhysicalForm.Type
	 ,UserMaster.FirstName+' '+LastName SenderName

      
  FROM [dbo].[Compliance] a 
     
		Join dbo.WasteMeasure b  on a.ComplianceFormID=b.ComplianceFormID
		join dbo.[ContractorAssessment] c on c.ContractorID=a.TransporterName
		join dbo.[ContractorAssessment] c1 on c1.ContractorID=a.ReceiverName
		join dbo.[UserMaster] on UserMaster.UserID=a.SenderCertificate 
		join dbo.VechicleType on VechicleType.VechicleId=a.TypeOfvechicle
		join dbo.PhysicalForm on PhysicalForm.PhsyicalFormId=a.PhysicalForm

	where a.ComplianceFormID=@ComplianceID



 
 







		
  

 










GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SelectContractAnnualRating]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SelectContractAnnualRating]
@Fromdate Varchar(15),
@Todate Varchar(15)
	

	AS
BEGIN
SET DATEFORMAT DMY
Declare @strFromDate as Varchar(100)
Set @strFromDate=Convert(Varchar(100),cast(@Fromdate as datetime))
Declare @strToDate as Varchar(100)
Set @strToDate=Convert(Varchar(100),cast(@Todate as datetime))

	SELECT CompanyName as ContractorName,
COUNT(ContractorRating) as TotalPermits,
sum(case when ContractorRating = 'Y' then 1 else 0 end)AS OrangePermits,
sum(case when ContractorRating = 'G' then 1 else 0 end)   as GreenPermits,
sum(case when ContractorRating = 'R' then 1 else 0 end) as RedPermits,
((sum(case when ContractorRating = 'G' then 1 else 0 end)*1+sum(case when ContractorRating = 'Y' then 1 else 0 end)*0+sum(case when ContractorRating = 'R' then 1 else 0 end)*-1)*100/ case when COUNT(ContractorRating)=0 then 1 else COUNT(ContractorRating)end) as TotalPercentage,
1 as Rank,
FrequencyName as AssessmentFrequency,
 c.AssessmentDate as LastAssessmentDate,
	  IIF(FrequencyName='6 Months',Cast(c.AssessmentDate+180 as Datetime),IIF(FrequencyName='12 Months',Cast(c.AssessmentDate+365 as Datetime),Cast(c.AssessmentDate+730 as Datetime))) NextAssessmentDate
 
 

from WorkPermit w
 join [ContractorAssessment] c on c.ContractorID=w.ContractorID
join ContractorFrequency on ContractorFrequency.FrequencyID=c.Frequency  
where cast(w.CreatedOn as datetime)  between @strFromDate and @strToDate

group by CompanyName , FrequencyName ,AssessmentDate





END








GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Selectpno1]
  AS
 BEGIN
    declare @pno1 int;
  SET @pno1 =(SELECT COUNT(Status)
   FROM WpsTest1.[dbo].[WorkPermit] WHERE Status='E');
   
   RETURN @pno1;
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[summa]
(
	@WorkTypeID int
)
AS
begin
 SET NOCOUNT ON;

declare @hotwork int
declare @csentry  int
declare @electrical  int
declare @nonelectrical  int
declare @unloadingchemical int
declare @mechanical  int
declare @civil  int
declare @excavation  int
declare @Firehydrant int
declare @Hfr  int
declare @Hvac int
declare @linebreaking int
declare @lototagout  int
declare @shifingmaterial  int
declare @plumbingwork int
declare @paintingwork  int
declare @others int


SELECT  
      @electrical=[Lotoelectrical]
      ,@nonelectrical=[Lotononelectrical]
      ,@excavation=[Excavation]
      ,@mechanical=[Mechanical]
      ,@Hvac=[Hvac]
      ,@hotwork=[Hotwork]
      ,@unloadingchemical=[LoadingUnloading]
      ,@Hfr=[HeightFragileroof]
      ,@civil=[Civilwork]
      ,@csentry=[CSEntry]
      ,@paintingwork=[Paintingwork]
      ,@Firehydrant=[Firehydrant]
      ,@plumbingwork=[Plumbingwork]
      ,@shifingmaterial=[Shitingmaterial]
      ,@lototagout=[Loto/Tagout]
      ,@linebreaking=[LineBreaking]
     ,@others=[others]

  FROM WpsTest1.[dbo].[TypeofWorkforCreatePermit] where WorkPermitID=@WorkTypeID

 
declare @hotworkkk int
declare @csentryyy  int
declare @electricalll  int
declare @nonelectricalll  int
declare @unloadingchemicalll int
declare @mechanicalll  int
declare @civilll  int

declare @Hfrrr  int
declare @Hvaccc int

declare @plumbingworkkk  int
declare @paintingworkkk  int
declare @othersss int

if(@hotwork>0)
 set @hotworkkk=1
 else
 set @hotworkkk=null
if( @csentry>0)
 set  @csentryyy=1
 else
 set @csentryyy=null
if(@electrical>0)
 set @electricalll=1
 else
 set @electricalll=null
if(@nonelectrical>0)
 set @nonelectricalll=1
 else
 set @nonelectricalll=null

 else
  set @mechanicalll=null

 set @civilll =1
 else
 set @civilll =null

 set @excavationnn=1
 else
 set @excavationnn=null
if(@Firehydrant>0)
 set @Firehydranttt=1
 else
  set @Firehydranttt=null
if(@Hfr>0)
 set @Hfrrr=1
 else
  set @Hfrrr=null
if(@Hvac>0)
 set @Hvaccc=1
 else
 set @Hvaccc=null
if(@linebreaking>0)
 set @linebreakinggg=1
 else
 set @linebreakinggg=null
if(@lototagout>0)
 set @lototagouttt=1
 else
 set @lototagouttt=null
if(@shifingmaterial>0)
 set @shifingmaterialll=1
 else
  set @shifingmaterialll=null
if(@plumbingwork>0)
 set @plumbingworkkk=1
 else
 set @plumbingworkkk=null
if(@paintingwork>0)
 set @paintingworkkk=1
 else
 set @paintingworkkk=null
 if(@others>0)
 set @othersss=1
 else
 set @othersss=null




    select  UserID ,  FirstName+' '+LastName UserFullName from UserMaster Where IsActive='Y' and UserID in(select UserID from PermitApprover where  Lotoelectrical=isnull(@electricalll,Lotoelectrical) and Lotononelectrical=isnull(@nonelectricalll,Lotononelectrical) and Excavation=isnull(@excavationnn,Excavation) and Mechanical=isnull(@mechanicalll,Mechanical) and Hvac=isnull(@Hvaccc,Hvac) and Hotwork=isnull(@hotworkkk,Hotwork) and LoadingUnloading=isnull(@unloadingchemicalll,LoadingUnloading) and HeightFragileroof=isnull(@Hfrrr,HeightFragileroof) and Civilwork=isnull(@civilll,Civilwork) and CSEntry=isnull(@csentryyy,CSEntry) and Paintingwork=isnull(@paintingworkkk,Paintingwork) and Firehydrant=isnull(@Firehydranttt,Firehydrant) and Plumbingwork=isnull(@plumbingworkkk,Plumbingwork) and Shitingmaterial=isnull(@shifingmaterialll,Shitingmaterial) and LineBreaking=ISNULL(@linebreakinggg,LineBreaking) and LockOutTagOut=ISNULL(@lototagouttt,LockOutTagOut)and others=ISNULL(@othersss,others ) )

  --select us.UserID, us.FirstName+''+us.LastName UserFullName from PermitApprover pa join UserMaster us on us.UserID=pa.UserID where

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TypeofWorkforCreatepermitInsert]
	@WorkPermitID int ,
	@Lotoelectrical int,
	@Lotononelectrical int,
	@LotoTagout int,
	@Excavation int,
	@Mechanical int,
	@Hvac int,
	@Hotwork int,
	@LoadingUnloading int,
	@HeightFragileroof int,
	@Civilwork int,
	@CSEntry int,
	@Paintingwork int,
	@Firehydrant int,
	@Plumbingwork int,
	@Shitingmaterial int,
	@LineBreaking int,
	@others int,
	@CreatedBy int
AS
BEGIN
	 Insert into TypeofWorkforCreatePermit
	 (WorkPermitID
      ,[Lotoelectrical]
      ,[Lotononelectrical]
      ,[Excavation]
      ,[Mechanical]
	  ,[Hvac]
      ,[Hotwork]
      ,[LoadingUnloading]
      ,[HeightFragileroof]
      ,[Civilwork]
      ,[CSEntry]
      ,[Paintingwork]
      ,[Firehydrant]
      ,[Plumbingwork]
      ,[Shitingmaterial]
	  ,[Loto/Tagout]
	  ,[LineBreaking]
      ,[others]
	  ,CreatedBy
	  ,CraetedOn)

	  values(@WorkPermitID
	  ,@Lotoelectrical
	  ,@Lotononelectrical
	  ,@Excavation
	  ,@Mechanical
	  ,@Hvac
	  ,@Hotwork
	  ,@LoadingUnloading
	  ,@HeightFragileroof
	  ,@Civilwork
	  ,@CSEntry
	  ,@Paintingwork
	  ,@Firehydrant
	  ,@Plumbingwork
	  ,@Shitingmaterial
	  ,@LotoTagout
	  ,@LineBreaking
	  ,@others
	  ,@CreatedBy
	  ,CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
	  )
 
END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TypeofWorkforCreatepermitUpdate]
 @WorkPermitID int ,
	@Lotoelectrical int,
	@Lotononelectrical int,
	@Excavation int,
	@Mechanical int,
	@Hvac int,
	@Hotwork int,
	@LoadingUnloading int,
	@HeightFragileroof int,
	@Civilwork int,
	@CSEntry int,
	@Paintingwork int,
	@Firehydrant int,
	@Plumbingwork int,
	@Shitingmaterial int,
	@LotoTagout int,
	@LineBreaking int,
	@others int,
	@LastUpdatedBy int
AS
BEGIN
update TypeofWorkforCreatePermit
set Lotoelectrical=@Lotoelectrical,
Lotononelectrical=@Lotononelectrical,
Excavation=@Excavation,
Mechanical=@Mechanical,
Hvac=@Hvac,
Hotwork=@Hotwork,
LoadingUnloading=@LoadingUnloading,
HeightFragileroof=@HeightFragileroof,
Civilwork=@Civilwork,
CSEntry=@CSEntry,
Paintingwork=@Paintingwork,
Firehydrant=@Firehydrant,
Plumbingwork=@Plumbingwork,
Shitingmaterial=@Shitingmaterial,
[Loto/Tagout]=@LotoTagout,
LineBreaking=@LineBreaking,
others=@others,
LastUpdatedBy=@LastUpdatedBy,
LastUpdatedOn=CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
 Where WorkPermitID=@WorkPermitID;

END

	  ,@LineBreaking
	  ,@LotoTagout

	  )

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[TypeofWorkUpdate]
 @ContractID int ,
	@Lotoelectrical int,
	@Lotononelectrical int,
	@Excavation int,
	@Mechanical int,
	@Hvac int,
	@Hotwork int,
	@LoadingUnloading int,
	@HeightFragileroof int,
	@Civilwork int,
	@CSEntry int,
	@Paintingwork int,
	@Firehydrant int,
	@Plumbingwork int,
	@Shitingmaterial int,
	@LineBreaking int,
	@Lototagout int,
	@others int,
	@LastUpdatedBy int
AS
BEGIN
update TypeofWorkChecklist
set Lotoelectrical=@Lotoelectrical,
Lotononelectrical=@Lotononelectrical,
Excavation=@Excavation,
Mechanical=@Mechanical,
Hvac=@Hvac,
Hotwork=@Hotwork,
LoadingUnloading=@LoadingUnloading,
HeightFragileroof=@HeightFragileroof,
Civilwork=@Civilwork,
CSEntry=@CSEntry,
Paintingwork=@Paintingwork,
Firehydrant=@Firehydrant,
Plumbingwork=@Plumbingwork,
Shitingmaterial=@Shitingmaterial,
LineBreaking=@LineBreaking,
LotoTagout=@Lototagout,
others=@others,
LastUpdatedBy=@LastUpdatedBy,
LastUpdatedOn=CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
 Where ContractorID=@ContractID;

END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UserMasterGet]
@UserID INT
AS
BEGIN
	select UserRoles.RoleID, 
	        UserRoles.FrequencyID,
			UserMaster.UserID,
			FirstName,
			LastName,
			EmailAddress,
			UserName,
			Password,
			MobileNo,
			Designation,
			Userimage,
			IsActive  from 	UserMaster
			 Join [UserRoles] on UserMaster.UserID=UserRoles.UserID 
		
			 where UserMaster.UserID=@UserID 

   SELECT [RoleID],[RoleName] from RoleMaster

END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

 
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UserMasterInsert]
(
@FirstName varchar(50),
@LastName  varchar(50),
@EmailAddress varchar(50),
@MobileNumber varchar(15),
@RoleID int,
@FrequencyID int,
@UserName  varchar(50),
@Password varchar(100),
@Designation varchar(50),
@CreatedBy int
)
AS
Begin
 Begin Try
 	
	if EXISTS  (select 1 from UserMaster where EmailAddress=@EmailAddress) 
    RAISERROR ('Email Already Exists',11,1);

	if Exists(select 1 from UserMaster where UserName=@UserName)
	RAISERROR ('UserName Already Exists',11,1);
	
 	Insert into UserMaster(FirstName,Lastname,EmailAddress,UserName,Password,Designation,MobileNo,IsActive,CreatedBy,CreatedOn)
	 Values(@FirstName,@LastName,@EmailAddress,lower(@UserName),@Password,@Designation,@MobileNumber,'Y',@CreatedBy, sysdatetime())
	
	Insert into  UserRoles Values(@@IDENTITY,@RoleID,@FrequencyID,@CreatedBy,sysdatetime(),SYSDATETIME())







	






End try
BEGIN CATCH
	  DECLARE @ErrorMessage VARCHAR(500);
	  SELECT  @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE() 
	  RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage,11,1);
END CATCH;

End













GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[UserMasterSelect]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UserMasterSelect]
AS
BEGIN
	select  a.UserID,
			FirstName,
			LastName,
			FirstName+' '+LastName DisplayUserName,
			EmailAddress,
			UserName,
			MobileNo,
			Designation,
			UserImage,
			case when IsActive='Y' THEN 'Yes' ELSE 'No' END IsActive,
			c.RoleName,
			f.FrequencyName
 from dbo.UserMaster a
 	    Left Join dbo.UserRoles b on a.UserID=b.UserID 
		Left Join dbo.RoleMaster c on c.RoleID=b.RoleID 
		left join FrequencyMaster f on b.FrequencyID=f.FrequencyID
 order by FirstName,LastName
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[UserMasterUpdate]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

 
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[UserMasterUpdate]
@UserID int,
@FirstName varchar(50),
@LastName   varchar(50),
@EmailAddress Varchar(50),
@MobileNo   Varchar(50),
@UserName Varchar(50),
@Password varchar(100),
@Designation varchar (50),
@UserImage varchar(100),
@RoleID int,
@FrequencyID int,
@IsActive    varchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
	Begin Try
	
	if EXISTS  (select 1 from UserMaster where EmailAddress=@EmailAddress and UserID!=@UserID) 
    RAISERROR (' Email Already Exists',11,1);
	if  Exists (select 1 from UserMaster where UserName=lower(@UserName) and UserID!=@UserID)
    RAISERROR ('UserName Already Exists',11,1);
	update UserMaster set Firstname=@FirstName ,LastName=@LastName,EmailAddress=@EmailAddress, 
	MobileNo=@MobileNo ,UserName=lower(@UserName),Password=@Password,Designation=@Designation,
	UserImage=case when @UserImage is not null then @UserImage else UserImage end,
	IsActive=@IsActive  where UserID=@UserID
 
   If (@RoleID is not null)
   Update UserRoles set RoleID=@RoleID,FrequencyID=@FrequencyID,LastUpdated=SYSDATETIME() where UserID=@UserID


 
 End try
BEGIN CATCH
	  DECLARE @ErrorMessage VARCHAR(500);
	  SELECT  @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE() 
	  RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage,11,1);
END CATCH;
 

END

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		 Chella
-- Create date: 23-Apr-2015
-- Description:	Stored procedure to Validate the User
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ValidateUser] 
@UserName Varchar(50),
@Password Varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
Select UserID,UserName,FirstName,LastName,FirstName+' '+LastName FullName,UserImage, Designation from 
UserMaster where IsActive='Y' And lower(UserName)=lower(@UserName) And Password=@Password;

Select RoleMaster.RoleID,RoleName from UserMaster users, UserRoles,RoleMaster Where  users.UserID=UserRoles.UserID 
and rolemaster.RoleID=UserRoles.roleid and IsActive='Y' and lower(UserName)=lower(@UserName) And Password=@Password;

END

GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WasteInsert] 
     @WasteNo int,
     @WasteTagId varchar(50),
     @WasteName varchar(100),
     @UoM varchar(100)

AS
Begin
    IF Exists(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.WasteList where WasteNo=@WasteNo )
RAISERROR ('WasteNo already exists.',11,1);
   
ELSE IF Exists(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.WasteList where WasteTagId=@WasteTagId)
RAISERROR ('WasteTagId already exists.',11,1);

ELSE IF Exists(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.WasteList where WasteName=@WasteName )
RAISERROR ('WasteName already exists.',11,1);
else


Insert into WasteList(WasteNo,WasteTagId,WasteName,UoM,CreatedOn,LastUpdateDatetime)
	 Values(@WasteNo,@WasteTagID,@WasteName,@UoM,SYSDATETIME(),SYSDATETIME())
	

End

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WasteQuantity]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WasteQuantity] 
@WasteMeasure xml,
@ComplianceFormID int

AS
BEGIN
 
INSERT INTO [dbo].WasteMeasure 
SELECT
  ComplianceFormID=@ComplianceFormID 
  
 ,WasteList.Field.value('WasteId[1]', 'nvarchar(10)')WasteId
 ,WasteList.Field.value('WasteName[1]','varchar(30)')WasteName
 ,WasteList.Field.value('Quantity[1]', 'varchar(30)')Quantity

,sysdatetime()  
FROM Compliance 
cross apply  @WasteMeasure.nodes('ArrayOfWasteQuantity/WasteQuantity') WasteList(Field)  where ComplianceFormID=@ComplianceFormID 


END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WasteQuantityUpdate]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

create PROCEDURE [dbo].[WasteQuantityUpdate] 
@WasteMeasure xml,
@ComplianceFormID int

AS
BEGIN
 
update WasteMeasure 
set
 Quantity=WasteList.Field.value('Quantity[1]', 'varchar(30)')
,CreatedOn=CURRENT_TIMESTAMP

FROM  @WasteMeasure.nodes('ArrayOfWasteQuantity/WasteQuantity') WasteList(Field)  where ComplianceFormID=@ComplianceFormID and 

WasteId=WasteList.Field.value('WasteId[1]', 'varchar(30)')

 

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WasteUpdate]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
 
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WasteUpdate] 
     @WasteId int,
	 @WasteNo int,
     @WasteTagId varchar(50),
     @WasteName varchar(100),
     @UoM varchar(100)
    
   AS
   BEGIN
     IF Exists(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.WasteList where WasteNo=@WasteNo and WasteId<>@WasteId)
RAISERROR ('WasteNo already exists.',11,1);
   
ELSE IF Exists(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.WasteList where WasteTagId=@WasteTagId and WasteId<>@WasteId)
RAISERROR ('WasteTagId already exists.',11,1);

ELSE IF Exists(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.WasteList where WasteName=@WasteName and WasteId<>@WasteId)
RAISERROR ('WasteName already exists.',11,1);
else


UPDATE [dbo].[WasteList]
   SET 
      [WasteNo] = @WasteNo,
      [WasteTagId] = @WasteTagId
      ,[WasteName] =@WasteName 
	  ,[UoM] =@UoM 
      ,[LastUpdateDateTime]=SYSDATETIME()
 WHERE WasteId=@WasteId
 

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WorkPermitForPDF]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WorkPermitForPDF]

	@WorkID int
AS
BEGIN
SELECT 
      a.WorkPermitID
      ,FORMAT([ValidityFrom] , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ValidityFrom
      ,FORMAT([ValidityTo] , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ValidityTo
      ,[Location]
      ,[EquipmentName]
       ,[CompanyName]
      ,[WorkDesctiption]
       ,case when [Lotoelectrical]=1 then'Electrical,'else'' end+
	  case when [Lotononelectrical]=1 then' Non-Electrical,'else'' end+case when [Excavation]=1 then' Excavation,'else''end+case when [Mechanical]=1 then' Mechanical,'else'' end
	  +case when [Hvac]=1 then' Hvac,'else''end+case when [Hotwork]=1 then' Hotwork,'else'' end+case when [LoadingUnloading]=1 then' UnloadingChemical,'else''end
	  +case when [HeightFragileroof]=1 then' HeightFragileroof,'else'' end+case when Civilwork=1 then' Civilwork,'else''end
	  +case when [CSEntry]=1 then' Confined Space Entry,'else'' end+case when [Paintingwork]=1 then' Paintingwork,'else''end
      +case when [Firehydrant]=1 then' Firehydrant,'else''end+case when [Plumbingwork]=1 then' Plumbingwork,'else'' end+case when [Shitingmaterial]=1 then'Shitingmaterial,'else''end
	  +case when [Loto/Tagout]=1 then' LockOut TagOut,'else'' end+case when [LineBreaking]=1 then' LineBreaking,'else''end
	  +case when [others]=1 then'others'else'' end as WorkTypeID
      ,[FireWatchRequired]
	  
      ,[PermitHolderName]
      ,[NoOfPersonAtSite]
      , Permit.FirstName+' '+Permit.LastName as Permitissuer
      ,adjacent.FirstName+' '+adjacent.LastName as [AdjacentAreaOwenerID]
      ,Approve.FirstName+' '+Approve.LastName as[ApproverID]
     , [PermitHolderName]
	  ,AcceptedAreaOwner.FirstName+' '+AcceptedAreaOwner.LastName as AcceptedAreaOwner
      ,FORMAT(ClosedOn , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ClosedOn
      ,[ContractorRating]
	  ,[ClosureComment]
	   ,a.Status
	    ,FORMAT(ex.ExtensionFrom , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ExtensionFrom
      ,FORMAT(ex.ExtensionTo , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ExtensionTo
      ,extensionIssuer.FirstName +' '+extensionIssuer.LastName as ExtensionIssuer
      ,extensionAreaOwner.FirstName +' '+extensionAreaOwner.LastName as ExtensionAreaOwner
      ,extensionApprover.FirstName +' '+extensionApprover.LastName as ExtensionApprover

     
    
	  ,[RiskAssessmentRequired]
	  ,f.PersonName+' '+f.PersonLastName  PersonName
      FROM  [dbo].[WorkPermit] a 
	  inner join UserMaster Permit on a.PermitIssuerID=Permit.UserID
      left join UserMaster  adjacent on a.AdjacentAreaOwenerID=adjacent.UserID
      join UserMaster Approve on a.ApproverID=Approve.UserID
	  
	 join EquipmentMaster e on a.EquipmentID=e.EquipmentID
	 join FireWatchPerson f on a.FireWatchRequired=f.PersonID
      Left join UserMaster  AcceptedAreaOwner on a.ClosureAreaOwnerID=AcceptedAreaOwner.UserID
      Left Join dbo.TypeofWorkforCreatePermit b on a.WorkPermitID=b.WorkPermitID
	  Left Join ContractorAssessment on a.ContractorID=ContractorAssessment.ContractorID
	  left join ExtensionPermit ex on ex.ExtensionPermitID=a.ExtensionPermitID
	  Left Join UserMaster extensionAreaOwner on ex.ExtensionAreaOwnerID =extensionAreaOwner.UserID
	  Left Join UserMaster extensionApprover on ex.ExtensionApproverID =extensionApprover.UserID
	  Left Join UserMaster extensionIssuer on ex.ExtensionPermitIssuerID =extensionIssuer.UserID
	  where a.WorkPermitID=@WorkID


	  SELECT [PPEId]
      ,[WorkPermitID]
      ,[HelmetWithChinStrip]
      ,[SplashGoggles]
      ,[EarPlugsMuff]
      ,[CottonHandGloves]
      ,[NitrileHandGloves]
      ,[HeatResistantHandGloves]
      ,[ElectricalGloves]
      ,[DustMask]
      ,[SolventMask]
      ,[FaceShield]
      ,[FullBodyHarness]
      ,[LifelineWithRatchet]
      ,[GumBoot]
      ,[ShoesWithNonConductiveSole]
      ,[RespiratoryProtection]
      ,[ChemicalProtectiveClothing]
      ,[Coveralls]
      ,[RescueEquipment]
      ,[TripodHoist]
      ,[Wristlets]
      ,[Scaffolding]
      ,[FallArrester]
      ,[SafetyBelt]
      ,[LadderCondition]
      ,[ESDRegular]
      ,[Others]
     
  FROM  [dbo].[PPE] where WorkPermitID=@WorkID

 SELECT  [TypeofWorkID]
      ,[WorkPermitID]
	  ,[Hotwork]
	   ,[LineBreaking]
	   ,[Loto/Tagout]
	   ,[LoadingUnloading]
	   ,[CSEntry]
      ,[Lotoelectrical]      
      ,[HeightFragileroof]     
	  ,[Excavation]
	  
	  
	
        FROM [dbo].[TypeofWorkforCreatePermit] where WorkPermitID=@WorkID

       
END














GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WorkPermitGet]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WorkPermitGet]
	
	@WorkPermitID int
AS
BEGIN

/****** Script for SelectTopNRows command from SSMS  ******/
SELECT w.[WorkPermitID]
     ,FORMAT([ValidityFrom] , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ValidityFrom
      ,FORMAT([ValidityTo] , 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss') ValidityTo
      ,[Location]
      ,[EquipmentID]
      ,[ContractorID]
      ,[WorkDesctiption]
      ,[WorkTypeID]
	  ,[RiskAssessmentRequired]
      ,[FireWatchRequired]
      ,[PermitHolderName]
      ,[NoOfPersonAtSite]
      ,[PermitIssuerID]
	  ,u.[FirstName]+' '+u.LastName PermitIssuerName
      ,[AdjacentAreaOwenerID]
      ,[ApproverID]
      ,[ClosurePermitHolderID]
      ,[ClosureAreaOwnerID]
      ,[ClosureDateTime]
      ,[ContractorRating]
      ,w.[CreatedBy]
      ,w.[CreatedOn]
      ,[Status]
	 ,[Attachment]
	 ,[WholeAttachment]
	 ,at.Attachement
      ,[ApproverComment]
      ,[ApprovedBy]

      ,[ApprovedOn]
      ,[PermitHolder]
      ,[AcceptedAreaOwner]
      ,[ClosureComment]
      ,[ClosedBy]
      ,[ClosedOn]
      ,[LastModifiedBy]
      ,[LastModifiedOn]
      ,[ClosurePermitHolderName]
      ,[ClosurePermitHolderSignedOn]
     
      ,[ClosureAreaOwnerSignedOn]
	
      ,[ClosureAreaOwnerSignedOn]
	  ,[ExtensionPermitID]

  FROM (([dbo].[WorkPermit] w
		full outer Join [dbo].[ApproveListAttachement] at on w.[WorkPermitID]=at.[WorkPermitId])
		join [dbo].UserMaster u on w.PermitIssuerID=u.UserID)
		
					Where w.[WorkPermitID]=@WorkPermitID 





  Exec [dbo].PPEGet @WorkPermitID
  Exec [dbo].[TypeofWorkGetforcreatepermit] @WorkPermitID
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WorkPermitInsert]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WorkPermitInsert] 
	@ValidityFrom datetime=null,
	@ValidityTo datetime=null,
	@Location varchar(50)=null,
	@EquipmentID int=0,
	@ContractorID int = 0,
	@WorkDesctiption varchar(1000)=null,
	@WorkTypeID int=0,
	@RiskAssessmentRequired int=0,
	@FireWatchRequired int=0,
	@PermitHolderName varchar(100) = 0,
	@NoOfPersonAtSite varchar(100)=0,
	@PermitIssuerID int = 0,
	@AdjacentAreaOwenerID int = 0,
	@ApproverID int = 0,
 	@CreatedBy int=0,
	@Status char(1) = 'D',
	@PermitID int output
AS
BEGIN
	SET DATEFORMAT DMY
INSERT INTO [dbo].[WorkPermit]
           ([ValidityFrom]
           ,[ValidityTo]
           ,[Location]
		   ,[EquipmentID]
           ,[ContractorID]
           ,[WorkDesctiption]
           ,[WorkTypeID]
		   ,[RiskAssessmentRequired]
           ,[FireWatchRequired]
           ,[PermitHolderName]
           ,[NoOfPersonAtSite]
           ,[PermitIssuerID]
           ,[AdjacentAreaOwenerID]
           ,[ApproverID]
           ,[CreatedBy]
		   ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[Status]
		   ,LastModifiedBy
		   ,LastModifiedOn)
     VALUES
           (@ValidityFrom, 
            @ValidityTo,
            @Location,
            @EquipmentID,
			@ContractorID,
			@WorkDesctiption,
			@WorkTypeID,
			@RiskAssessmentRequired,
			@FireWatchRequired,
			@PermitHolderName, 
			@NoOfPersonAtSite, 
			@PermitIssuerID,
			@AdjacentAreaOwenerID,
			@ApproverID,
 			@CreatedBy,
			CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
			@Status,
			@CreatedBy,
			CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
			)
			Set @PermitId=@@IDENTITY
  END


 










GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[WorkPermitUpdate]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WorkPermitUpdate]
@WorkPermitID int,
@ValidityFrom datetime=null,
@ValidityTo datetime=null,
@Location varchar(50)=null,
@EquipmentID int=0,
@ContractorID int = 0,
@WorkDesctiption varchar(1000)=null,
@WorkTypeID int=0,
@RiskAssessmentRequired int=0,
@FireWatchRequired int=0,
@PermitHolderName varchar(100) = null,
@NoOfPersonAtSite varchar(100) = null,
@PermitIssuerID int=0,
@AdjacentAreaOwenerID int=0,
@ApproverID int=0,
@Status char(1)=null,
@LastModifiedBy int =0 
AS
BEGIN


UPDATE [dbo].[WorkPermit]
   SET [ValidityFrom] = @ValidityFrom 
      ,[ValidityTo] = @ValidityTo
      ,[Location] = @Location
      ,[EquipmentID] = @EquipmentID
      ,[ContractorID] = @ContractorID
      ,[WorkDesctiption] = @WorkDesctiption
      ,[WorkTypeID] = @WorkTypeID
	  ,[RiskAssessmentRequired]=@RiskAssessmentRequired
      ,[FireWatchRequired] = @FireWatchRequired
      ,[PermitHolderName] = @PermitHolderName
      ,[NoOfPersonAtSite] = @NoOfPersonAtSite
      ,[PermitIssuerID] = @PermitIssuerID
      ,[AdjacentAreaOwenerID] = @AdjacentAreaOwenerID
      ,[ApproverID] = @ApproverID
      ,[Status] = @Status
	       ,[LastModifiedBy]=@LastModifiedBy
	  ,[LastModifiedOn]=CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
 WHERE WorkPermitID=@WorkPermitID
   
END











GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[WorkPermitUpdateStatus]
@WorkPermitID int,
@Status char(1)=null,
@Attachment varchar(100),
@LastModifiedBy int =0 
AS
BEGIN


UPDATE [dbo].[WorkPermit]

	  ,[LastModifiedOn]=CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
 WHERE WorkPermitID=@WorkPermitID
   
END

/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetDueDate]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date, ,>
-- Description:	<Description, ,>
-- =============================================
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetDueDate]
(
@UserID int
)
RETURNS varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
	 
DECLARE @Frequency Varchar(15)
DECLARE @CompleteDate datetime


select @Frequency=FrequencyName from UserRoles join FrequencyMaster on UserRoles.FrequencyID=FrequencyMaster.FrequencyID
 where  UserID=@UserID

 

    SELECT TOP 1 @CompleteDate=isnull(CompleteDate,'') FROM [dbo].[PermitReview] WHERE UserID=@UserID and FrequencyName=@Frequency ORDER BY CompleteDate desc
  


If (@Frequency='Daily')	 
	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",1,@CompleteDate), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Weekly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",7,@CompleteDate), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Monthly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",30,@CompleteDate), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Quarterly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",90,@CompleteDate),  'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Half Yearly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",180,@CompleteDate),  'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Yearly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",335,@CompleteDate),  'dd/MM/yyyy')
 
  	return @CompleteDate

end











GO
/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetRecentDueDate]    Script Date: 6/4/2019 11:23:16 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date, ,>
-- Description:	<Description, ,>
-- =============================================
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetRecentDueDate]
(
@UserID int
)
RETURNS varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
	 
DECLARE @Frequency Varchar(15)
DECLARE @CompleteDate datetime
DECLARE @FrequencyUpdated Datetime

select @Frequency=FrequencyName from UserRoles join FrequencyMaster on UserRoles.FrequencyID=FrequencyMaster.FrequencyID
 where  UserID=@UserID

   SELECT TOP 1 @CompleteDate=CompleteDate FROM [dbo].[PermitReview] WHERE UserID=@UserID and FrequencyName=@Frequency ORDER BY CompleteDate desc
  
  SELECT @FrequencyUpdated=isnull(@CompleteDate,LastUpdated)  from UserRoles where  UserID=@UserID ORDER BY LastUpdated desc

  

If (@Frequency='Daily')	 
	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",1,@FrequencyUpdated), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Weekly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",7,@FrequencyUpdated), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Monthly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",30,@FrequencyUpdated), 'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Quarterly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",90,@FrequencyUpdated),  'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Half Yearly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",180,@FrequencyUpdated),  'dd/MM/yyyy')
If (@Frequency='Yearly')
   	RETURN  FORMAT(DATEADD("d",335,@FrequencyUpdated),  'dd/MM/yyyy')

	
	 	return @FrequencyUpdated


end
